getNumericValue

  • getNumericValue(code: number): number
    • Defined in lib/CharUnicodeInfo.ts:67

    Data derived from https://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/#UnicodeData.txt. If Numeric_Type=Decimal or Numeric_Type=Digit or Numeric_Type=Numeric, then retrieves the Numeric_Value for this code point. Otherwise returns -1. This data is encoded in field 8 of UnicodeData.txt.
